59 /** Representation of the [[Request]] URI
60   *
61   * @param scheme     optional Uri Scheme. eg, http, https
62   * @param authority  optional Uri Authority. eg, localhost:8080, www.foo.bar
63   * @param path       url-encoded string representation of the path component of the Uri.
64   * @param query      optional Query. url-encoded.
65   * @param fragment   optional Uri Fragment. url-encoded.
66   */
67 final case class Uri(
68     scheme: Option[Uri.Scheme] = None,
69     authority: Option[Uri.Authority] = None,
70     path: Uri.Path = Uri.Path.empty,
71     query: Query = Query.empty,
72     fragment: Option[Uri.Fragment] = None,
73 ) extends QueryOps
74     with Renderable {
75 
76   /** Adds the path exactly as described. Any path element must be urlencoded ahead of time.
77     * @param path the path string to replace
78     */
79   @deprecated("Use {withPath(Uri.Path)} instead", "0.22.0-M1")
80   def withPath(path: String): Uri = copy(path = Uri.Path.unsafeFromString(path))
81 
82   def withPath(path: Uri.Path): Uri = copy(path = path)
83 
84   def withFragment(fragment: Uri.Fragment): Uri = copy(fragment = Option(fragment))
85 
86   def withoutFragment: Uri = copy(fragment = Option.empty[Uri.Fragment])
87 
88   /** Urlencodes and adds a path segment to the Uri
89     *
90     * @param newSegment the segment to add.
91     * @return a new uri with the segment added to the path
92     */
93   def addSegment(newSegment: String): Uri = addSegment[String](newSegment)
94 
95   /** Urlencodes and adds a path segment to the Uri
96     *
97     * @tparam Type to be encoded to a Uri Segment
98     * @param newSegment the segment to add.
99     * @return a new uri with the segment added to the path
100     */
101   def addSegment[A: Uri.Path.SegmentEncoder](newSegment: A): Uri =
102     copy(path = path / newSegment)
103 
104   /** This is an alias to [[addSegment(*]]
105     */
106   def /(newSegment: String): Uri = addSegment[String](newSegment)
107 
108   /** This is an alias to [[addSegment[*]]]
109     */
110   def /[A: Uri.Path.SegmentEncoder](newSegment: A): Uri = addSegment[A](newSegment)
111 
112   /** Splits the path segments and adds each of them to the path url-encoded.
113     * A segment is delimited by /
114     * @param morePath the path to add
115     * @return a new uri with the segments added to the path
116     */
117   def addPath(morePath: String): Uri =
118     copy(path = morePath.split("/").foldLeft(path)((p, segment) => p.addSegment(segment)))
119 
120   def host: Option[Uri.Host] = authority.map(_.host)
121   def port: Option[Int] = authority.flatMap(_.port)
122   def userInfo: Option[Uri.UserInfo] = authority.flatMap(_.userInfo)
123 
124   def resolve(relative: Uri): Uri = Uri.resolve(this, relative)
125 
126   /** Representation of the query string as a map
127     *
128     * In case a parameter is available in query string but no value is there the
129     * sequence will be empty. If the value is empty the the sequence contains an
130     * empty string.
131     *
132     * =====Examples=====
133     * <table>
134     * <tr><th>Query String</th><th>Map</th></tr>
135     * <tr><td><code>?param=v</code></td><td><code>Map("param" -> Seq("v"))</code></td></tr>
136     * <tr><td><code>?param=</code></td><td><code>Map("param" -> Seq(""))</code></td></tr>
137     * <tr><td><code>?param</code></td><td><code>Map("param" -> Seq())</code></td></tr>
138     * <tr><td><code>?=value</code></td><td><code>Map("" -> Seq("value"))</code></td></tr>
139     * <tr><td><code>?p1=v1&amp;p1=v2&amp;p2=v3&amp;p2=v3</code></td><td><code>Map("p1" -> Seq("v1","v2"), "p2" -> Seq("v3","v4"))</code></td></tr>
140     * </table>
141     *
142     * The query string is lazily parsed. If an error occurs during parsing
143     * an empty `Map` is returned.
144     */
145   def multiParams: Map[String, immutable.Seq[String]] = query.multiParams
146 
147   /** View of the head elements of the URI parameters in query string.
148     *
149     * In case a parameter has no value the map returns an empty string.
150     *
151     * @see multiParams
152     */
153   def params: Map[String, String] = query.params
154 
155   override lazy val renderString: String =
156     super.renderString
157 
158   override def render(writer: Writer): writer.type = {
159     def renderScheme(s: Uri.Scheme): writer.type =
160       writer << s << ':'
161 
162     this match {
163       case Uri(Some(s), Some(a), _, _, _) =>
164         renderScheme(s) << "//" << a
165 
166       case Uri(Some(s), None, _, _, _) =>
167         renderScheme(s)
168 
169       case Uri(None, Some(a), _, _, _) =>
170         writer << "//" << a // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/64513631/uri-and-double-slashes/64513776#64513776
171 
172       case Uri(None, None, _, _, _) =>
173     }
174 
175     this match {
176       case Uri(_, Some(_), p, _, _) if p.nonEmpty && !p.absolute =>
177         writer << "/" << p
178       case Uri(None, None, p, _, _) =>
179         if (!p.absolute && p.segments.headOption.fold(false)(_.toString.contains(":"))) {
180           writer << "./" << p // https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc3986#section-4.2 last paragraph
181         } else {
182           writer << p
183         }
184       case Uri(_, _, p, _, _) =>
185         writer << p
186     }
187 
188     if (query.nonEmpty) writer << '?' << query
189     fragment.foreach { f =>
190       writer << '#' << Uri.encode(f, spaceIsPlus = false)
191     }
192     writer
193   }
194 
195   // ///////// Query Operations ///////////////
196   override protected type Self = Uri
197 
198   override protected def self: Self = this
199 
200   override protected def replaceQuery(query: Query): Self = copy(query = query)
201 
202   /** Converts this request to origin-form, which is the absolute path and optional
203     * query.  If the path is relative, it is assumed to be relative to the root.
204     */
205   def toOriginForm: Uri =
206     Uri(path = path.toAbsolute, query = query)
207 }
208 
209 object Uri extends UriPlatform {
210 
211   /** Decodes the String to a [[Uri]] using the RFC 3986 uri decoding specification */
212   def fromString(s: String): ParseResult[Uri] =
213     ParseResult.fromParser(Parser.uriReferenceUtf8, "Invalid URI")(s)
214 
215   /** Parses a String to a [[Uri]] according to RFC 3986.  If decoding
216     *  fails, throws a [[ParseFailure]].
217     *
218     *  For totality, call [[fromString]].  For compile-time
219     *  verification of literals, call [[uri]].
220     */
221   def unsafeFromString(s: String): Uri =
222     fromString(s).valueOr(throw _)
223 
224   /** Decodes the String to a [[Uri]] using the RFC 7230 section 5.3 uri decoding specification */
225   def requestTarget(s: String): ParseResult[Uri] =
226     ParseResult.fromParser(Parser.requestTargetParser, "Invalid request target")(s)
227 
228   /** A [[org.http4s.Uri]] may begin with a scheme name that refers to a
229     * specification for assigning identifiers within that scheme.
230     *
231     * If the scheme is defined, the URI is absolute.  If the scheme is
232     * not defined, the URI is a relative reference.
233     *
234     * @see [[https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc3986#section-3.1 RFC 3986, Section 3.1, Scheme]]
235     */
236   final class Scheme private[http4s] (val value: String) extends Ordered[Scheme] {
237     override def equals(o: Any): Boolean =
238       o match {
239         case that: Scheme => this.value.equalsIgnoreCase(that.value)
240         case _ => false
241       }
242 
243     private[this] var hash = 0
244     override def hashCode(): Int = {
245       if (hash == 0)
246         hash = hashLower(value)
247       hash
248     }
249 
250     override def toString: String = s"Scheme($value)"
251 
252     override def compare(other: Scheme): Int =
253       value.compareToIgnoreCase(other.value)
254   }
255 
256   object Scheme {
257     val http: Scheme = new Scheme("http")
258     val https: Scheme = new Scheme("https")
259 
260     @deprecated("Renamed to fromString", "0.21.0-M2")
261     def parse(s: String): ParseResult[Scheme] = fromString(s)
262 
263     def fromString(s: String): ParseResult[Scheme] =
264       ParseResult.fromParser(Parser.scheme, "Invalid scheme")(s)
265 
266     /** Like `fromString`, but throws on invalid input */
267     def unsafeFromString(s: String): Scheme =
268       fromString(s).fold(throw _, identity)
269 
270     implicit val http4sOrderForScheme: Order[Scheme] =
271       Order.fromComparable
272     implicit val http4sShowForScheme: Show[Scheme] =
273       Show.fromToString
274     implicit val http4sInstancesForScheme: HttpCodec[Scheme] =
275       new HttpCodec[Scheme] {
276         def parse(s: String): ParseResult[Scheme] =
277           Scheme.fromString(s)
278 
279         def render(writer: Writer, scheme: Scheme): writer.type =
280           writer << scheme.value
281       }
282   }
283 
284   type Fragment = String
285 
286   final case class Authority(
287       userInfo: Option[UserInfo] = None,
288       host: Host = RegName("localhost"),
289       port: Option[Int] = None,
290   ) extends Renderable {
291     override def render(writer: Writer): writer.type =
292       this match {
293         case Authority(Some(u), h, None) => writer << u << '@' << h
294         case Authority(Some(u), h, Some(p)) => writer << u << '@' << h << ':' << p
295         case Authority(None, h, Some(p)) => writer << h << ':' << p
296         case Authority(_, h, _) => writer << h
297       }
298   }
299 
300   object Authority {
301 
302     implicit val catsInstancesForHttp4sAuthority
303         : Hash[Authority] with Order[Authority] with Show[Authority] =
304       new Hash[Authority] with Order[Authority] with Show[Authority] {
305         override def hash(x: Authority): Int =
306           x.hashCode
307 
308         override def compare(x: Authority, y: Authority): Int = {
309           def compareAuthorities[A: Order](focus: Authority => A): Int =
310             compareField(x, y, focus)
311 
312           reduceComparisons(
313             compareAuthorities(_.userInfo),
314             Eval.later(compareAuthorities(_.host)),
315             Eval.later(compareAuthorities(_.port)),
316           )
317         }
318 
319         override def show(a: Authority): String =
320           a.renderString
321       }
322   }
323 
324   final class Path private (
325       val segments: Vector[Path.Segment],
326       val absolute: Boolean,
327       val endsWithSlash: Boolean,
328   ) extends Renderable {
329 
330     def isEmpty: Boolean = segments.isEmpty
331     def nonEmpty: Boolean = segments.nonEmpty
332 
333     override def equals(obj: Any): Boolean =
334       obj match {
335         case p: Path => doEquals(p)
336         case _ => false
337       }
338 
339     private def doEquals(path: Path): Boolean =
340       this.segments == path.segments && path.absolute == this.absolute && path.endsWithSlash == this.endsWithSlash
341 
342     override def hashCode(): Int = {
343       var hash = segments.hashCode()
344       hash += 31 * absolute.hashCode()
345       hash += 31 * endsWithSlash.hashCode()
346       hash
347     }
348 
349     def render(writer: Writer): writer.type = {
350       val start = if (absolute) "/" else ""
351       writer << start << segments.iterator.mkString("/")
352       if (endsWithSlash && segments.nonEmpty) writer << "/" else writer
353     }
354 
355     override val renderString: String = super.renderString
356     override def toString: String = renderString
357 
358     /** This is an alias to [[addSegment(*]]
359       */
360     def /(segment: Path.Segment): Path = addSegment(segment)
361 
362     /** This is an alias to [[addSegment[*]]
363       */
364     def /[A: Path.SegmentEncoder](segment: A): Path = addSegment[A](segment)
365 
366     def addSegment(segment: Path.Segment): Path = addSegments(List(segment))
367     def addSegment[A](segment: A)(implicit encoder: Path.SegmentEncoder[A]): Path =
368       addSegments(List(encoder.toSegment(segment)))
369 
370     def addSegments(value: Seq[Path.Segment]): Path =
371       Path(this.segments ++ value, absolute = absolute || this.segments.isEmpty)
372 
373     def normalize: Path = Path(segments.filterNot(_.isEmpty))
374 
375     /* Merge paths per RFC 3986 5.2.3 */
376     def merge(path: Path): Path = {
377       val merge = if (isEmpty) segments else segments.init
378       Path(merge ++ path.segments, absolute = absolute, endsWithSlash = path.endsWithSlash)
379     }
380 
381     def concat(path: Path): Path =
382       Path(
383         segments ++ path.segments,
384         absolute = this.absolute || (this.isEmpty && path.absolute),
385         endsWithSlash = path.endsWithSlash || (path.isEmpty && this.endsWithSlash),
386       )
387 
388     def startsWith(path: Path): Boolean = segments.startsWith(path.segments)
389 
390     def startsWithString(path: String): Boolean = startsWith(Path.unsafeFromString(path))
391 
392     @deprecated("Misnamed, use findSplit(prefix) instead", since = "0.22.0-M1")
393     def indexOf(prefix: Path): Option[Int] = findSplit(prefix)
394 
395     @deprecated("Misnamed, use findSplitOfString(prefix) instead", since = "0.22.0-M1")
396     def indexOfString(path: String): Option[Int] = findSplit(Path.unsafeFromString(path))
397 
398     def findSplit(prefix: Path): Option[Int] =
399       if (startsWith(prefix)) Some(prefix.segments.size)
400       else None
401     def findSplitOfString(path: String): Option[Int] = findSplit(Path.unsafeFromString(path))
402 
403     def splitAt(idx: Int): (Path, Path) =
404       if (idx <= 0) {
405         (Path.empty, this)
406       } else if (idx < segments.size) {
407         val (start, end) = segments.splitAt(idx)
408         (
409           Path(start, absolute = absolute),
410           Path(end, absolute = true, endsWithSlash = endsWithSlash),
411         )
412       } else if (idx == segments.size) {
413         (Path(segments, absolute = absolute), if (endsWithSlash) Path.Root else Path.empty)
414       } else {
415         (this, Path.empty)
416       }
417     private def copy(
418         segments: Vector[Path.Segment] = segments,
419         absolute: Boolean = absolute,
420         endsWithSlash: Boolean = endsWithSlash,
421     ): Path = Path(segments, absolute, endsWithSlash)
422 
423     def dropEndsWithSlash: Path = copy(endsWithSlash = false)
424     def addEndsWithSlash: Path = copy(endsWithSlash = true)
425 
426     def toAbsolute: Path = copy(absolute = true)
427     def toRelative: Path = copy(absolute = false)
428   }
429 
430   object Path {
431     val empty: Path = new Path(Vector.empty, absolute = false, endsWithSlash = false)
432     val Root: Path = new Path(Vector.empty, absolute = true, endsWithSlash = true)
433     lazy val Asterisk: Path =
434       new Path(Vector(Segment("*")), absolute = false, endsWithSlash = false)
435 
436     final class Segment private (val encoded: String) {
437       def isEmpty = encoded.isEmpty
438 
439       override def equals(obj: Any): Boolean =
440         obj match {
441           case s: Segment => s.encoded == encoded
442         }
443 
444       override def hashCode(): Int = encoded.hashCode
445 
446       def decoded(
447           charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8,
448           plusIsSpace: Boolean = false,
449           toSkip: Char => Boolean = Function.const(false),
450       ): String =
451         Uri.decode(encoded, charset, plusIsSpace, toSkip)
452 
453       override val toString: String = encoded
454     }
455 
456     object Segment extends (String => Segment) {
457       def apply(value: String): Segment = new Segment(pathEncode(value))
458       def encoded(value: String): Segment = new Segment(value)
459 
460       val empty: Segment = Segment("")
461 
462       implicit val http4sInstancesForSegment: Order[Segment] =
463         new Order[Segment] {
464           def compare(x: Segment, y: Segment): Int =
465             x.encoded.compare(y.encoded)
466         }
467     }
468 
469     trait SegmentEncoder[A] extends Serializable {
470       def toSegment(a: A): Segment
471 
472       final def contramap[B](f: B => A): SegmentEncoder[B] =
473         b => this.toSegment(f(b))
474     }
475 
476     object SegmentEncoder {
477       def apply[A](implicit segmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[A]): SegmentEncoder[A] =
478         segmentEncoder
479 
480       def instance[A](f: A => Segment): SegmentEncoder[A] = f.apply _
481 
482       def fromToString[A]: SegmentEncoder[A] = v => Segment(v.toString())
483       def fromShow[A](implicit show: Show[A]): SegmentEncoder[A] =
484         v => Segment(show.show(v))
485 
486       implicit val segmentSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Segment] = identity[Segment] _
487 
488       implicit val charSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Char] = fromToString
489       implicit val stringSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[String] = Segment.apply _
490 
491       implicit val booleanSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Boolean] = fromToString
492 
493       implicit val byteSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Byte] = fromToString
494       implicit val shortSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Short] = fromToString
495       implicit val intSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Int] = fromToString
496       implicit val longSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Long] = fromToString
497       implicit val bigIntSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[BigInt] = fromToString
498 
499       implicit val floatSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Float] = fromToString
500       implicit val doubleSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[Double] = fromToString
501       implicit val bigDecimalSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[BigDecimal] = fromToString
502 
503       implicit val uuidSegmentEncoder: SegmentEncoder[java.util.UUID] = fromToString
504 
505       implicit val contravariantInstance: Contravariant[SegmentEncoder] =
506         new Contravariant[SegmentEncoder] {
507           override def contramap[A, B](fa: SegmentEncoder[A])(f: B => A): SegmentEncoder[B] =
508             fa.contramap(f)
509         }
510     }
511 
512     /** This constructor allows you to construct the path directly.
513       * Each path segment needs to be encoded for it to be used here.
514       *
515       * @param segments the segments that this path consists of. MUST be Urlencoded.
516       * @param absolute if the path is absolute. I.E starts with a "/"
517       * @param endsWithSlash if the path is a "directory", ends with a "/"
518       * @return a Uri.Path that can be used in Uri, or by itself.
519       */
520     def apply(
521         segments: Vector[Segment],
522         absolute: Boolean = false,
523         endsWithSlash: Boolean = false,
524     ): Path =
525       // make sure that we never end up with Path(Vector(), true, true) or Path(Vector(), false, true)
526       if (segments.isEmpty && (absolute || endsWithSlash)) Root
527       else new Path(segments, absolute, endsWithSlash)
528 
529     // def unapply(path: Path): Some[(Vector[Segment], Boolean, Boolean)] =
530     //   Some((path.segments, path.absolute, path.endsWithSlash))
531 
532     @deprecated(message = "Use unsafeFromString instead", since = "0.22.0-M6")
533     def fromString(fromPath: String): Path =
534       unsafeFromString(fromPath)
535 
536     def unsafeFromString(fromPath: String): Path =
537       fromPath match {
538         case "" => empty
539         case "/" => Root
540         case pth =>
541           val absolute = pth.startsWith("/")
542           val relative = if (absolute) pth.substring(1) else pth
543           Path(
544             segments = relative
545               .split("/")
546               .foldLeft(Vector.empty[Segment])((path, segment) => path :+ Segment.encoded(segment)),
547             absolute = absolute,
548             endsWithSlash = relative.endsWith("/"),
549           )
550       }
551 
552     implicit val http4sInstancesForPath: Order[Path] with Semigroup[Path] =
553       new Order[Path] with Semigroup[Path] {
554         def compare(x: Path, y: Path): Int = {
555           def comparePaths[A: Order](focus: Path => A): Int =
556             compareField(x, y, focus)
557           reduceComparisons(
558             comparePaths(_.absolute),
559             Eval.later(comparePaths(_.segments)),
560             Eval.later(comparePaths(_.endsWithSlash)),
561           )
562         }
563 
564         def combine(x: Path, y: Path): Path = x.concat(y)
565       }
566 
567   }
568 
569   /** The userinfo subcomponent may consist of a user name and,
570     * optionally, scheme-specific information about how to gain
571     * authorization to access the resource.  The user information, if
572     * present, is followed by a commercial at-sign ("@") that delimits
573     * it from the host.
574     *
575     * @param username The username component, decoded.
576     *
577     * @param password The password, decoded.  Passing a password in
578     * clear text in a URI is a security risk and deprecated by RFC
579     * 3986, but preserved in this model for losslessness.
580     *
581     * @see [[https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc3986#section-3.2.1 RFC 3986, Section 3.2.1, User Information]]
582     */
583   final case class UserInfo private ( // scalafix:ok Http4sGeneralLinters.nonValidatingCopyConstructor; bincompat until 1.0
584       username: String,
585       password: Option[String],
586   ) extends Ordered[UserInfo] {
587     override def compare(that: UserInfo): Int =
588       username.compareTo(that.username) match {
589         case 0 => Ordering.Option[String].compare(password, that.password)
590         case cmp => cmp
591       }
592   }
593 
594   object UserInfo {
595 
596     /** Parses a userInfo from a percent-encoded string. */
597     def fromString(s: String): ParseResult[UserInfo] =
598       fromStringWithCharset(s, StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
599 
600     /** Parses a userInfo from a string percent-encoded in a specific charset. */
601     def fromStringWithCharset(s: String, cs: JCharset): ParseResult[UserInfo] =
602       ParseResult.fromParser(Parser.userinfo(cs), "Invalid userinfo")(s)
603 
604     implicit val http4sInstancesForUserInfo
605         : HttpCodec[UserInfo] with Order[UserInfo] with Hash[UserInfo] with Show[UserInfo] =
606       new HttpCodec[UserInfo] with Order[UserInfo] with Hash[UserInfo] with Show[UserInfo] {
607         def parse(s: String): ParseResult[UserInfo] =
608           UserInfo.fromString(s)
609         def render(writer: Writer, userInfo: UserInfo): writer.type = {
610           writer << encodeUsername(userInfo.username)
611           userInfo.password.foreach(writer << ":" << encodePassword(_))
612           writer
613         }
614 
615         private val SkipEncodeInUsername =
616           Unreserved ++ "!$&'()*+,;="
617 
618         private def encodeUsername(s: String, charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8): String =
619           encode(s, charset, false, SkipEncodeInUsername)
620 
621         private val SkipEncodeInPassword =
622           SkipEncodeInUsername ++ ":"
623 
624         private def encodePassword(s: String, charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8): String =
625           encode(s, charset, false, SkipEncodeInPassword)
626 
627         def compare(x: UserInfo, y: UserInfo): Int = x.compareTo(y)
628 
629         def hash(x: UserInfo): Int = x.hashCode
630 
631         def show(x: UserInfo): String = x.toString
632       }
633   }
634 
635   sealed trait Host extends Renderable {
636     def value: String
637 
638     override def render(writer: Writer): writer.type =
639       this match {
640         case RegName(n) => writer << encode(n.toString)
641         case a: Ipv4Address => writer << a.value
642         case a: Ipv6Address => writer << '[' << a << ']'
643       }
644 
645     def toIpAddress: Option[ip4s.IpAddress] = this match {
646       case Ipv4Address(a) => Some(a)
647       case Ipv6Address(a) => Some(a)
648       case RegName(_) => None
649     }
650   }
651 
652   object Host {
653 
654     /** Create a [[Host]] value from an [[com.comcast.ip4s.IpAddress]].
655       *
656       * This is a convenience method for creating the correct host based on
657       * the underlying IP protocol version of the given address, either IPv4
658       * or IPv6.
659       */
660     def fromIpAddress(value: ip4s.IpAddress): Host =
661       value match {
662         case value: ip4s.Ipv4Address =>
663           Ipv4Address(value)
664         case value: ip4s.Ipv6Address =>
665           Ipv6Address(value)
666       }
667 
668     implicit val catsInstancesForHttp4sUriHost: Hash[Host] with Order[Host] with Show[Host] =
669       new Hash[Host] with Order[Host] with Show[Host] {
670         override def hash(x: Host): Int =
671           x match {
672             case x: Ipv4Address =>
673               x.hash
674             case x: Ipv6Address =>
675               x.hash
676             case x: RegName =>
677               x.hash
678           }
679 
680         override def compare(x: Host, y: Host): Int =
681           (x, y) match {
682             case (x: Ipv4Address, y: Ipv4Address) =>
683               x.compare(y)
684             case (x: Ipv6Address, y: Ipv6Address) =>
685               x.compare(y)
686             case (x: RegName, y: RegName) =>
687               x.compare(y)
688 
689             // Differing ADT constructors
690             // Ipv4Address is arbitrarily considered > all Ipv6Address and RegName
691             case (_: Ipv4Address, _) =>
692               1
693             case (_, _: Ipv4Address) =>
694               -1
695 
696             // Ipv6Address is arbitrarily considered > all RegName
697             case (_: Ipv6Address, _) =>
698               1
699             case (_, _: Ipv6Address) =>
700               -1
701           }
702 
703         override def show(a: Host): String =
704           a.renderString
705       }
706   }

877   /** Resolve a relative Uri reference, per RFC 3986 sec 5.2
878     */
879   def resolve(base: Uri, reference: Uri): Uri = {
880     val target = (base, reference) match {
881       case (_, Uri(Some(_), _, _, _, _)) => reference
882       case (Uri(s, _, _, _, _), Uri(_, a @ Some(_), p, q, f)) => Uri(s, a, p, q, f)
883       case (Uri(s, a, p, q, _), Uri(_, _, pa, Query.empty, f)) if pa.isEmpty => Uri(s, a, p, q, f)
884       case (Uri(s, a, p, _, _), Uri(_, _, pa, q, f)) if pa.isEmpty => Uri(s, a, p, q, f)
885       case (Uri(s, a, bp, _, _), Uri(_, _, p, q, f)) =>
886         if (p.absolute) Uri(s, a, p, q, f)
887         else Uri(s, a, bp.merge(p), q, f)
888     }
889 
890     target.withPath(removeDotSegments(target.path))
891   }
892 
893   /** Remove dot sequences from a Path, per RFC 3986 Sec 5.2.4
894     * Adapted from"
895     * https://github.com/Norconex/commons-lang/blob/c83fdeac7a60ac99c8602e0b47056ad77b08f570/norconex-commons-lang/src/main/java/com/norconex/commons/lang/url/URLNormalizer.java#L429
896     */
897   def removeDotSegments(path: Uri.Path): Uri.Path = {
898     // (Bulleted comments are from RFC3986, section-5.2.4)
899 
900     // 1.  The input buffer is initialized with the now-appended path
901     //     components and the output buffer is initialized to the empty
902     //     string.
903     val in = new StringBuilder(path.renderString)
904     val out = new StringBuilder
905 
906     // 2.  While the input buffer is not empty, loop as follows:
907     while (in.nonEmpty)
908       // A.  If the input buffer begins with a prefix of "../" or "./",
909       //     then remove that prefix from the input buffer; otherwise,
910       if (startsWith(in, "../"))
911         deleteStart(in, "../")
912       else if (startsWith(in, "./"))
913         deleteStart(in, "./")
914 
915       // B.  if the input buffer begins with a prefix of "/./" or "/.",
916       //     where "." is a complete path segment, then replace that
917       //     prefix with "/" in the input buffer; otherwise,
918       else if (startsWith(in, "/./"))
919         replaceStart(in, "/./", "/")
920       else if (equalStrings(in, "/."))
921         replaceStart(in, "/.", "/")
922 
923       // C.  if the input buffer begins with a prefix of "/../" or "/..",
924       //     where ".." is a complete path segment, then replace that
925       //     prefix with "/" in the input buffer and remove the last
926       //     segment and its preceding "/" (if any) from the output
927       //     buffer; otherwise,
928       else if (startsWith(in, "/../")) {
929         replaceStart(in, "/../", "/")
930         removeLastSegment(out)
931       } else if (equalStrings(in, "/..")) {
932         replaceStart(in, "/..", "/")
933         removeLastSegment(out)
934       }
935 
936       // D.  if the input buffer consists only of "." or "..", then remove
937       //      that from the input buffer; otherwise,
938       else if (equalStrings(in, ".."))
939         deleteStart(in, "..")
940       else if (equalStrings(in, "."))
941         deleteStart(in, ".")
942 
943       // E.  move the first path segment in the input buffer to the end of
944       //     the output buffer, including the initial "/" character (if
945       //     any) and any subsequent characters up to, but not including,
946       //     the next "/" character or the end of the input buffer.
947       else
948         in.indexOf("/", 1) match {
949           case nextSlashIndex if nextSlashIndex > -1 =>
950             out.append(in.substring(0, nextSlashIndex))
951             in.delete(0, nextSlashIndex)
952           case _ =>
953             out.append(in)
954             in.setLength(0)
955         }
956 
957     // 3.  Finally, the output buffer is returned as the result of
958     //     remove_dot_segments.
959     Uri.Path.unsafeFromString(out.toString)
960   }
961 
962   // Helper functions for removeDotSegments
963   private def startsWith(b: StringBuilder, str: String): Boolean =
964     b.indexOf(str) == 0
965   private def equalStrings(b: StringBuilder, str: String): Boolean =
966     b.length == str.length && startsWith(b, str)
967   private def deleteStart(b: StringBuilder, str: String): StringBuilder =
968     b.delete(0, str.length)
969   private def replaceStart(b: StringBuilder, target: String, replacement: String): StringBuilder = {
970     deleteStart(b, target)
971     b.insert(0, replacement)
972   }
973   private def removeLastSegment(b: StringBuilder): Unit =
974     b.lastIndexOf("/") match {
975       case -1 => b.setLength(0)
976       case n => b.setLength(n)
977     }
978 
979   private[http4s] def Unreserved = UriCoding.Unreserved
980 
981   /** Percent-encodes a string.  Depending on the parameters, this method is
982     * appropriate for URI or URL form encoding.  Any resulting percent-encodings
983     * are normalized to uppercase.
984     *
985     * @param toEncode the string to encode
986     * @param charset the charset to use for characters that are percent encoded
987     * @param spaceIsPlus if space is not skipped, determines whether it will be
988     * rendreed as a `"+"` or a percent-encoding according to `charset`.
989     * @param toSkip a predicate of characters exempt from encoding.  In typical
990     * use, this is composed of all Unreserved URI characters and sometimes a
991     * subset of Reserved URI characters.
992     */
993   def encode(
994       toEncode: String,
995       charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8,
996       spaceIsPlus: Boolean = false,
997       toSkip: Char => Boolean = toSkip,
998   ): String =
999     UriCoding.encode(toEncode, charset, spaceIsPlus, toSkip)
1000 
1001   private lazy val toSkip =
1002     UriCoding.Unreserved ++ "!$&'()*+,;=:/?@"
1003 
1004   private lazy val SkipEncodeInPath =
1005     UriCoding.Unreserved ++ ":@!$&'()*+,;="
1006 
1007   def pathEncode(s: String, charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8): String =
1008     encode(s, charset, false, SkipEncodeInPath)
1009 
1010   /** Percent-decodes a string.
1011     *
1012     * @param toDecode the string to decode
1013     * @param charset the charset of percent-encoded characters
1014     * @param plusIsSpace true if `'+'` is to be interpreted as a `' '`
1015     * @param toSkip a predicate of characters whose percent-encoded form
1016     * is left percent-encoded.  Almost certainly should be left empty.
1017     */
1018   def decode(
1019       toDecode: String,
1020       charset: JCharset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8,
1021       plusIsSpace: Boolean = false,
1022       toSkip: Char => Boolean = Function.const(false),
1023   ): String =
1024     if (toDecode.indexOf('%') < 0) {
1025       if (plusIsSpace && toDecode.indexOf('+') >= 0) toDecode.replace('+', ' ')
1026       else toDecode
1027     } else {
1028       val in = CharBuffer.wrap(toDecode)
1029       // reserve enough space for 3-byte UTF-8 characters.  4-byte characters are represented
1030       // as surrogate pairs of characters, and will get a luxurious 6 bytes of space.
1031       val out = ByteBuffer.allocate(in.remaining() * 3)
1032       while (in.hasRemaining) {
1033         val mark = in.position()
1034         val c = in.get()
1035         if (c == '%') {
1036           if (in.remaining() >= 2) {
1037             val xc = in.get()
1038             val yc = in.get()
1039             val x = Character.digit(xc, 0x10)
1040             val y = Character.digit(yc, 0x10)
1041             if (x != -1 && y != -1) {
1042               val oo = (x << 4) + y
1043               if (!toSkip(oo.toChar)) {
1044                 out.put(oo.toByte)
1045               } else {
1046                 out.put('%'.toByte)
1047                 out.put(xc.toByte)
1048                 out.put(yc.toByte)
1049               }
1050             } else {
1051               out.put('%'.toByte)
1052               in.position(mark + 1)
1053             }
1054           } else {
1055             // This is an invalid encoding. Fail gracefully by treating the '%' as
1056             // a literal.
1057             out.put(c.toByte)
1058             while (in.hasRemaining) out.put(in.get().toByte)
1059           }
1060         } else if (c == '+' && plusIsSpace) {
1061           out.put(' '.toByte)
1062         } else {
1063           // normally `out.put(c.toByte)` would be enough since the url is %-encoded,
1064           // however there are cases where a string can be partially decoded
1065           // so we have to make sure the non us-ascii chars get preserved properly.
1066           if (toSkip(c)) {
1067             out.put(c.toByte)
1068           } else {
1069             out.put(charset.encode(String.valueOf(c)))
1070           }
1071         }
1072       }
1073       out.flip()
1074       charset.decode(out).toString
1075     }
1076 
1077   implicit val catsInstancesForHttp4sUri: Hash[Uri] with Order[Uri] with Show[Uri] =
1078     new Hash[Uri] with Order[Uri] with Show[Uri] {
1079       override def hash(x: Uri): Int =
1080         x.hashCode
1081 
1082       override def compare(x: Uri, y: Uri): Int = {
1083         def compareUris[A: Order](focus: Uri => A): Int =
1084           compareField(x, y, focus)
1085 
1086         reduceComparisons(
1087           compareUris(_.scheme),
1088           Eval.later(compareUris(_.authority)),
1089           Eval.later(compareUris(_.path)),
1090           Eval.later(compareUris(_.query)),
1091           Eval.later(compareUris(_.fragment)),
1092         )
1093       }
1094 
1095       override def show(t: Uri): String =
1096         t.renderString
1097     }
1098 
1099   private[http4s] object Parser {
1100     /* port        = *DIGIT
1101      *
1102      * Limitation: we only parse up to Int. The spec allows bigint!
1103      */
1104     private[http4s] val port: Parser0[Option[Int]] = {
1105       import Rfc3986.digit
1106 
1107       digit.rep0.string.mapFilter {
1108         case "" => Some(None)
1109         case s =>
1110           try Some(Some(s.toInt))
1111           catch { case _: NumberFormatException => None }
1112       }
1113     }
1114 
1115     /* reg-name    = *( unreserved / pct-encoded / sub-delims) */
1116     private[http4s] val regName: Parser0[Uri.RegName] = {
1117       import Rfc3986.{pctEncoded, subDelims, unreserved}
1118 
1119       unreserved
1120         .orElse(pctEncoded)
1121         .orElse(subDelims)
1122         .rep0
1123         .string
1124         .map(s => Uri.RegName(CIString(Uri.decode(s))))
1125     }
1126 
1127     private[http4s] val ipv6Address: P[Uri.Ipv6Address] =
1128       Rfc3986.ipv6Address.map(Uri.Ipv6Address(_))
1129 
1130     private[http4s] val ipv4Address: P[Uri.Ipv4Address] =
1131       Rfc3986.ipv4Address.map(Uri.Ipv4Address(_))
1132 
1133     /* host          = IP-literal / IPv4address / reg-name */
1134     private[http4s] val host: Parser0[Uri.Host] = {
1135       import cats.parse.Parser.char
1136 
1137       // TODO This isn't in the 0.21 model.
1138       /* IPvFuture     = "v" 1*HEXDIG "." 1*( unreserved / sub-delims / ":" ) */
1139       val ipVFuture: P[Nothing] = P.fail
1140 
1141       /* IP-literal    = "[" ( IPv6address / IPvFuture  ) "]" */
1142       val ipLiteral = char('[') *> ipv6Address.orElse(ipVFuture) <* char(']')
1143 
1144       ipLiteral.orElse(ipv4Address.backtrack).orElse(regName)
1145     }
1146 
1147     /* userinfo    = *( unreserved / pct-encoded / sub-delims / ":" ) */
1148     private[http4s] def userinfo(cs: JCharset): Parser0[Uri.UserInfo] = {
1149       import cats.parse.Parser.{char, charIn, oneOf}
1150       import Rfc3986.{pctEncoded, subDelims, unreserved}
1151 
1152       val username = oneOf(unreserved :: pctEncoded :: subDelims :: Nil).rep0.string
1153       val password = oneOf(unreserved :: pctEncoded :: subDelims :: charIn(':') :: Nil).rep0.string
1154       (username ~ (char(':') *> password).?).map { case (u, p) =>
1155         Uri.UserInfo(Uri.decode(u, cs), p.map(Uri.decode(_, cs)))
1156       }
1157     }
1158 
1159     /* segment       = *pchar */
1160     private[http4s] val segment: Parser0[Uri.Path.Segment] =
1161       Rfc3986.pchar.rep0.string.map(Uri.Path.Segment.encoded)
1162 
1163     /* segment-nz    = 1*pchar */
1164     private[http4s] val segmentNz: P[Uri.Path.Segment] =
1165       Rfc3986.pchar.rep.string.map(Uri.Path.Segment.encoded)
1166 
1167     /* segment-nz-nc = 1*( unreserved / pct-encoded / sub-delims / "@" )
1168                    ; non-zero-length segment without any colon ":" */
1169     private[http4s] val segmentNzNc: P[Uri.Path.Segment] =
1170       Rfc3986.unreserved
1171         .orElse(Rfc3986.pctEncoded)
1172         .orElse(Rfc3986.subDelims)
1173         .orElse(P.char('@'))
1174         .rep
1175         .string
1176         .map(Uri.Path.Segment.encoded(_))
1177 
1178     import cats.parse.Parser.{char, pure}
1179 
1180     /* path-abempty  = *( "/" segment ) */
1181     private[http4s] val pathAbempty: Parser0[Uri.Path] =
1182       (char('/') *> segment).rep0.map {
1183         case Nil => Uri.Path.empty
1184         case List(Uri.Path.Segment.empty) => Uri.Path.Root
1185         case segments =>
1186           val segmentsV = segments.toVector
1187           if (segmentsV.last.isEmpty)
1188             Uri.Path(segmentsV.dropRight(1), absolute = true, endsWithSlash = true)
1189           else
1190             Uri.Path(segmentsV, absolute = true, endsWithSlash = false)
1191       }
1192 
1193     /* path-absolute = "/" [ segment-nz *( "/" segment ) ] */
1194     private[http4s] val pathAbsolute: P[Uri.Path] =
1195       (char('/') *> (segmentNz ~ (char('/') *> segment).rep0).?).map {
1196         case Some((head, tail)) =>
1197           val segmentsV = head +: tail.toVector
1198           if (segmentsV.last.isEmpty)
1199             Uri.Path(segmentsV.dropRight(1), absolute = true, endsWithSlash = true)
1200           else
1201             Uri.Path(segmentsV, absolute = true, endsWithSlash = false)
1202         case None =>
1203           Uri.Path.Root
1204       }
1205 
1206     /* path-rootless = segment-nz *( "/" segment ) */
1207     private[http4s] val pathRootless: P[Uri.Path] =
1208       (segmentNz ~ (char('/') *> segment).rep0).map { case (head, tail) =>
1209         val segmentsV = head +: tail.toVector
1210         if (segmentsV.last.isEmpty)
1211           Uri.Path(segmentsV.dropRight(1), absolute = false, endsWithSlash = true)
1212         else
1213           Uri.Path(segmentsV, absolute = false, endsWithSlash = false)
1214       }
1215 
1216     /* path-empty    = 0<pchar> */
1217     private[http4s] val pathEmpty: Parser0[Uri.Path] =
1218       pure(Uri.Path.empty)
1219 
1220     /* path-noscheme = segment-nz-nc *( "/" segment ) */
1221     private[http4s] val pathNoscheme: P[Uri.Path] =
1222       (segmentNzNc ~ (char('/') *> segment).rep0).map { case (head, tail) =>
1223         val segmentsV = head +: tail.toVector
1224         if (segmentsV.last.isEmpty)
1225           Uri.Path(segmentsV.dropRight(1), absolute = false, endsWithSlash = true)
1226         else
1227           Uri.Path(segmentsV, absolute = false, endsWithSlash = false)
1228       }
1229 
1230     /* absolute-path = 1*( "/" segment ) */
1231     private[http4s] val absolutePath: P[Uri.Path] =
1232       (char('/') *> segment).rep.map {
1233         case NonEmptyList(Uri.Path.Segment.empty, Nil) => Uri.Path.Root
1234         case segments =>
1235           val segmentsV = segments.toList.toVector
1236           if (segmentsV.last.isEmpty)
1237             Uri.Path(segmentsV.dropRight(1), absolute = true, endsWithSlash = true)
1238           else
1239             Uri.Path(segmentsV, absolute = true, endsWithSlash = false)
1240       }
1241 
1242     /* authority   = [ userinfo "@" ] host [ ":" port ] */
1243     private[http4s] def authority(cs: JCharset): Parser0[Uri.Authority] =
1244       ((userinfo(cs) <* char('@')).backtrack.? ~ host ~ (char(':') *> port).?).map {
1245         case ((ui, h), p) => Uri.Authority(userInfo = ui, host = h, port = p.flatten)
1246       }
1247 
1248     /* fragment    = *( pchar / "/" / "?" )
1249      *
1250      * Not URL decoded.
1251      */
1252     private[http4s] val fragment: Parser0[Uri.Fragment] =
1253       Rfc3986.pchar.orElse(P.charIn("/?")).rep0.string
1254 
1255     /* scheme      = ALPHA *( ALPHA / DIGIT / "+" / "-" / "." ) */
1256     private[http4s] val scheme: P[Uri.Scheme] = {
1257       import cats.parse.Parser.{charIn, not, string}
1258       import Rfc3986.{alpha, digit}
1259 
1260       val unary = alpha.orElse(digit).orElse(charIn("+-."))
1261 
1262       (string("https") <* not(unary))
1263         .as(Uri.Scheme.https)
1264         .backtrack
1265         .orElse((string("http") <* not(unary)).as(Uri.Scheme.http))
1266         .backtrack
1267         .orElse((alpha *> unary.rep0).string.map(new Uri.Scheme(_)))
1268     }
1269 
1270     /* request-target = origin-form
1271                       / absolute-form
1272                       / authority-form
1273                       / asterisk-form
1274      */
1275     private[http4s] val requestTargetParser: Parser0[Uri] = {
1276       import cats.parse.Parser.{char, oneOf0}
1277       import Query.{parser => query}
1278 
1279       /* origin-form    = absolute-path [ "?" query ] */
1280       val originForm: P[Uri] =
1281         (absolutePath ~ (char('?') *> query).?).map { case (p, q) =>
1282           Uri(scheme = None, authority = None, path = p, query = q.getOrElse(Query.empty))
1283         }
1284 
1285       /* absolute-form = absolute-URI */
1286       def absoluteForm: P[Uri] = absoluteUri(StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
1287 
1288       /* authority-form = authority */
1289       val authorityForm: Parser0[Uri] =
1290         authority(StandardCharsets.UTF_8).map(a => Uri(authority = Some(a)))
1291 
1292       /* asterisk-form = "*" */
1293       val asteriskForm: P[Uri] =
1294         char('*').as(Uri(path = Uri.Path.Asterisk))
1295 
1296       oneOf0(originForm :: absoluteForm :: authorityForm :: asteriskForm :: Nil)
1297     }
1298 
1299     /* hier-part   = "//" authority path-abempty
1300      *             / path-absolute
1301      *             / path-rootless
1302      *             / path-empty
1303      */
1304     def hierPart(cs: JCharset): Parser0[(Option[Uri.Authority], Uri.Path)] = {
1305       import P.string
1306       val rel: P[(Option[Uri.Authority], Uri.Path)] =
1307         (string("//") *> authority(cs) ~ pathAbempty).map { case (a, p) =>
1308           (Some(a), p)
1309         }
1310       P.oneOf0(
1311         rel :: pathAbsolute.map((None, _)) :: pathRootless.map((None, _)) :: pathEmpty.map(
1312           (None, _)
1313         ) :: Nil
1314       )
1315     }
1316 
1317     /* absolute-URI  = scheme ":" hier-part [ "?" query ] */
1318     private[http4s] def absoluteUri(cs: JCharset): P[Uri] = {
1319       import cats.parse.Parser.char
1320       import Query.{parser => query}
1321 
1322       (scheme ~ (char(':') *> hierPart(cs)) ~ (char('?') *> query).?).map { case ((s, (a, p)), q) =>
1323         Uri(scheme = Some(s), authority = a, path = p, query = q.getOrElse(Query.empty))
1324       }
1325     }
1326 
1327     private[http4s] def uri(cs: JCharset): P[Uri] = {
1328       import cats.parse.Parser.char
1329       import Query.{parser => query}
1330 
1331       (scheme ~ (char(':') *> hierPart(cs)) ~ (char('?') *> query).? ~ (char('#') *> fragment).?)
1332         .map { case (((s, (a, p)), q), f) =>
1333           Uri(
1334             scheme = Some(s),
1335             authority = a,
1336             path = p,
1337             query = q.getOrElse(Query.empty),
1338             fragment = f,
1339           )
1340         }
1341     }
1342 
1343     /* relative-part = "//" authority path-abempty
1344                      / path-absolute
1345                      / path-noscheme
1346                      / path-empty
1347      */
1348     private[http4s] def relativePart(cs: JCharset): Parser0[(Option[Uri.Authority], Uri.Path)] = {
1349       import cats.parse.Parser.string
1350 
1351       P.oneOf0(
1352         (string("//") *> authority(cs) ~ pathAbempty).map { case (a, p) =>
1353           (Some(a), p)
1354         } :: (pathAbsolute
1355           .map((None, _))) :: (pathNoscheme.map((None, _))) :: (pathEmpty.map((None, _))) :: Nil
1356       )
1357     }
1358 
1359     /* relative-ref  = relative-part [ "?" query ] [ "#" fragment ] */
1360     private[http4s] def relativeRef(cs: JCharset): Parser0[Uri] = {
1361       import cats.parse.Parser.char
1362       import Query.{parser => query}
1363 
1364       (relativePart(cs) ~ (char('?') *> query).? ~ (char('#') *> fragment).?).map {
1365         case (((a, p), q), f) =>
1366           Uri(
1367             scheme = None,
1368             authority = a,
1369             path = p,
1370             query = q.getOrElse(Query.empty),
1371             fragment = f,
1372           )
1373       }
1374     }
1375 
1376     private[http4s] val uriReferenceUtf8: Parser0[Uri] = uriReference(StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
1377     private[http4s] def uriReference(cs: JCharset): Parser0[Uri] =
1378       uri(cs).backtrack.orElse(relativeRef(cs))
1379   }
